<h2>Out of Africa</h2>

<p>Out of Africa</a> is a <a href="http://www.outofafrica.com.au/about.html" target="_blank">multi-award winning</a>, authentic Moroccan restaurant. Head Chef, Hassan M'Souli has opened many Moroccan restaurants since relocating from Casablanca in 1985, and even received a plaque from the Moroccan government in 2008 in recognition of his contribution to the promotion of Moroccan culture in Australia. The menu consists of exotic and aromatic dishes that pay homage to traditional influences.</p>

<h2 id="emperors-garden-bbq">Emperor’s Garden BBQ</h2>

<p>Emperor’s Garden BBQ, centrally located in Haymarket, specialises in authentic Hong Kong cuisine. A family-owned business for over 10 years, the Emperor’s Garden chain of restaurants was a City of Sydney Business Award finalist</a> in 2009, 2010, 2011 and 2012.</p>

<h2 id="ratings--reviews">Ratings &amp; Reviews</h2>

<div style="display: block"><table align="center"><tbody><tr>


<td style="width: 150px" align="center"><a href="http://www.urbanspoon.com/r/70/750782/restaurant/Chinatown/Emperors-Garden-BBQ-Sydney" target="_blank"><font color="#333333">Urbanspoon</font></a>
<div style="background-image: url('http://box.groupon-australia.net/editorial/images/stars.gif'); width: 80px; height: 80px; position: relative;"><div style="width: 80px; height: 80px; position: absolute; top: 30px; font: 12pt Arial, sans-serif; font-weight: bold; text-align: center;">77%</div></div></td>



</tr></tbody></table></div>

<blockquote>
Emperor's Garden BBQ Noodles is the old school Hong Kong style of Chinese restaurant we love so dearly. Inside is decor schmecor, plain and simple but with plenty of room to swing a chopstick. There's a touch of formality to the dagginess: waiters in white shirts, a small wine list, which makes this joint a pleasant yet casual spot where we've often ended  up with visitors and family over the years. It's a special kind of place.
<br /><a href="http://www.urbanspoon.com/r/70/750782/restaurant/Chinatown/Emperors-Garden-BBQ-Sydney" target="_blank">Street Food, Urbanspoon, December 2013</a>
</blockquote>

<blockquote>
Good place to eat, nice and quick

<h2>Bona Fides Cafe Restaurant</h2>

<p>Located on Druitt Street in the midst of Sydney’s bustling CBD, Bona Fides Cafe Restaurant</a> offers a range of modern Australian cuisine. Early risers can treat themselves to a morning meal with breakfast options including grilled mushrooms on toast, bacon and eggs and the Brazilian breakfast served with scrambled eggs and chorizo. Folks looking for lunch and dinner can silence grumbling bellies with meals such as Tasmanian smoked salmon salad, Wagyu bolognaise spaghetti and veal parmigiana.</p>

<h4 id="the-boutique-collectionbr-br-">The Boutique Collection<br /><br /></h4>

<p>Choose from over forty hand-picked luxury properties in Cairns, Palm Cove and Port Douglas, with options including hotel rooms, apartments, villas and homes to suit any preference. Poolside, beachside, suites, and retreats are all available in resort-style accommodation handpicked for their quality, warmth, and comfort. <p>While no two properties are the same, The Boutique Collection can offer advice on which properties would best suit the needs of holidaymakers. The company provides linen and beach towels, and can also organise additional extras, such as a daily service for those looking for an extra touch of luxury. </p>

<h4 id="north-queenslandbr-br-">North Queensland<br /><br /></h4>

<p>From vibrant Cairns and the Great Barrier Reef, to the stunning Cassowary Coast, the natural heritage and parks of Port Douglas, and the breathtaking Daintree Rainforest, far north Queensland has a lot to offer visitors. The coast is home to a bounty of unforgettable sites and experiences, both natural and man-made. Make sure to hit the Esplanade in Cairns; the buzzing and bustling heart of the city. Markets, BBQs, picnics, live music and shops can all be found around the quintessential walk along the waterfront. Party late at one of the many stylish bars with jaw-dropping views of the water, or have a quiet moment watching the sun rise over Trinity Bay. Take in an awe-inspiring wonder of the world in the Great Barrier Reef before taking in the more earthly wonders at Botanical Gardens on Collins Street. </p>

<p><img src="http://img.grouponcdn.com/deal/dAFVXEpt4da2UymW7d4v/Wb-700x400" width="472" height="300" /></p>

<p>The lush green rolling hills of the Aterton tablelands with their freshwater falls and townships steeped in history are often regarded as ‘the’ Australian experience. There isn’t much that hasn’t already been written about hauntingly beautiful glory of the most remarkable natural wonder of the world, the Great Barrier Reef. The Cassowary Coast boasts some of Australia’s most beautiful coastline and bushwalks, while the lush Daintree Rainforest is over 135 million years old and a World Heritage listed site.</p>

<h2>Cheeky Czech</h2>

<p>Cheeky Czech </a> is a small family run restaurant in the heart of Newtown serving breakfast, lunch and dinner. Cheeky Czech aims to serve fresh, authentic tasting food in a fun, comfortable and relaxed setting. Dishes served include salt and pepper calamari, Czech potato fritters, bread dumplings, farm rabbit, stuffed peppers and crumbled mushroom cups. See the full <a href="http://www.cheekyczech.com.au/file/files/Cheeky%20Czech%20Beer%20Cafe%20Menu.pdf" target="_blank">menu </a> here. </p>

<h2 id="in-asia">In Asia</h2>

<p>In Asia</a> serves pan-Asian fusion cuisine, prepared using fresh Australian produce. The menu features a taco of shredded Gochujang chicken breast with 
sesame and pickled cucumber, crispy skin salmon served with In Asia’s spiced kumara mash, cashew nuts and sweet potato chips and chargrilled wagyu rump with chilli flakes and lime sauce. The bar serves a variety of exotic cocktails and mocktails, including the Pa-ngan (chilli-infused Bacardi, Malibu, coconut cream, pineapple juice and lime), the Bali (Havana Club, fresh coconut juice, Pandanus syrup, lime and mint) and the Dragon (vodka, triple sec, fresh passionfruit, brown sugar, mint and soda). 
Dine in and delivery are available.</p>

<h2>Na Bangkok</h2>

<p>Na Bangkok specialises in Thai street food prepared with fresh ingredients. Specialities include a variety of rotis, the ever-popular grilled skewers, and classic Thai curries. Dine in and delivery are available. </p>

<blockquote>
this place is unlike any other I've been, they have a nice variety of dishes including roti (never seen this at Thai before!).
all the dishes we ordered were quite tasty. definitely loving the Hainan style chicken rice they do.
<br /><a href="http://www.urbanspoon.com/r/70/1504213/restaurant/Sydney/Na-Bangkok-Maroubra" target="_blank">Facebook User, Urbanspoon, January 2014</a>
</blockquote>

<blockquote>
I've been going to Na Bangkok for nearly 2 years and the quality of food and its standard has never dropped. One of my favourite dishes is the Kau Kai with chilli sauce which I can never seem to find in any other Thai restaurants in Sydney. This place is an absolute treasure and the service is always good. Highly recommended!!
<br /><a href="http://www.urbanspoon.com/r/70/1504213/restaurant/Sydney/Na-Bangkok-Maroubra" target="_blank">Mademoiselle_Vii, Urbanspoon, September 2013</a>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Arial, sans-serif; color: #333333; text-align: justify; line-height: 20px;">Offering people an extra line of defence against unwanted glare and stares, <font color="#339933">Tint Ur Ride</font></a> offers window tinting treatments for cars, homes and offices. Treatments for commercial windows include things like frosting on office partitions, security film, anti-graffiti film and reflective chrome tinting to help keep the heat at bay. Residential options are designed to safeguard privacy and help cut down on air conditioning bills by controlling the home’s temperature. A range of car services are available in addition to window tinting including electronic rust protection, paint protection, vinyl protection and leather protection.</p>
